689458494487247_689460331153730	948536071833123	2015-05-07T05:45:08+0000	Possession of Flats delayed in 72% of 6.45l NCR flats.

NEW DELHI: Living in their own home - and not a rented accommodation - remains an endless wait and dream for lakhs of people who booked residential units in the NCR. 

Over 72% of the 6.45 lakh homes that were supposed to be handed over to buyers by 2013 are delayed by anywhere from two to four years.

According to realty analysts the average delay in possession is 29 to 30 months in Noida.The result: Scores of middle class families struggling to pay both rent of their rented homes and EMIs for the ones they bought for a long time in these very difficult and expensive times.

The problem is most severe in the Noida region where almost 3.2 lakh of the 3.6 lakh homes - or 88.7% units - that were supposed to have been delivered by  2013 are inordinately delayed by up to three years.

"The biggest builders names have been the worst performers here and the single biggest reason, say realty experts and property dealers, is the builders' greed to grow where money collected from home buyers of one project is not used to complete that project but to launch several other projects eventually leaving all of them hanging.

Flat buyers are badly suffering by paying both rent and EMIs. A flat booked in Noida way back in 2010 the delivery was promised within three years. Now the builder says we may get our home next year. How painful ?

The government or courts must take some serious actions against such builders as meeting family expenses after paying EMI and rent is becoming increasingly tougher for the flat buyer.

What's worse  there is no real recourse available to harried home buyers as  governments seem to side with influential builders and leave the flat buyers to their fate. "

While Mr Rahul Gandhi heard the pain of the common man with regard to above now people are waiting for outcome of his hearing as builders are laughing at buyers.

688780234555073_688819131217850	993379794019761	2015-05-05T12:06:20+0000	IS WASTE BEING WASTED? It is often not discussed that urine contains 11-1-2% respectively of N-P-K (Sodium-Phosphorous-Potassium) which if properly harvested can be a good source of fertilizer for agriculture which the government currently subsidizes. An average person voids 350-700ml of urine 4-7 times a day. The normal range is 800 to 2000 milliliters per day with a normal fluid intake [www.nlm.nih.gov/medlineplus/ ency/article/ 003425.htm] [en.wikipedia.org/ wiki/ Fluid balance] Human urine being acidic can to an extent be used in alkaline soil. A dairy cow excretes 25 liters urine/day or 9000 liters annually. This urine being alkaline can be highly useful for correcting (acidic) soil. Solid human and animal wastes are a source of energy and manure. China   had 685,000 separation toilets spread among 17 provinces in 2003. China uses pigs in community toilets for sanitation and waste utilisation. They also add the water hyacinth for feeding pigs. In India a system where pigs scavenge open latrine is prevalent in some pockets. There is ample scope to explore the role of animals and the use of animal waste management for sustainable sanitation through scientific veterinary intervention. Use of manure gas (Gobar gas) though limited (0.3% & 0.1%) is an eco-friendly a method that need be considered and improved to suit each region. There is scope to explore the role of animals and the use of animal waste management for sustainable sanitation through scientific intervention.
When urine and solid waste are mixed, they start to ferment. In the Separation toilet no such process occurs and unpleasant smell is less. Separation toilet produces the most fertile fertilizer. The separation is used to recycle the solid waste back to nature as biogas and organic fertilizer. The process inactivates human pathogens so that the waste can be composted harmlessly. Handling the liquid is easy. It is mixed with eight parts water to make good fertilizer for garden! Large sewage system, certainly not flushing water is needed; it is a benefit to the environment

Sir
With due respect and humble submission I wish to laydown the following few lines for your kind consideration and favorable action please.
I am an Ex-Serviceman retired form indian army after serving a tenure of 15 years and I lost my one leg during my service.
I have some land dispute with vijay and others in my village and an order to maintain status-quo is given by Allahabad high court in my favour.
In this land dispute vijay and others as per FIR no 514041 beaten me with lathi and danda on 29 March 2015 and beaten my whole family who came to save me and they continue to beat me until they were assured that I am died. I was serious and admitted to ICU Ward of Heritage Hospital Varansi from 29 Mar 15 to 15 april 2015.
On the same day when i was beaten with my whole family and everybody was busy in taking treatment in the hospital the police registered a fasle FIR against my whole family member under IPC 452 including me and started to arrest my family members and on the other side did not register a FIR against vijay and others.
On the next day my son who is serving with army contacted with his officers and and when his commanding officer called to SP ballia then a simple case of fighting was registered against vijay and others.
On the next day my wife contacted with SHO Rasra and asked for the copy of FIR but he told my wife that FIR is not written till the time come in the evening and I will give you and when my wife went on next day he made other excuses after one day my son told DIG office Azamgarh, IG Varanasi and DGP control room uttar Pradesh but still he made exuses and did not provide the copy of FIR . on the next day my son called to DGP control room and took on conference with my wife and told the onduty officer to talk with DGP control room when DGP control room scolded the on duty officer he immediately gave the copy of the FIR but after providing the copy of FIR he told my son that who are you when you will come on leave I will see you and did not allow my wife to leave the police station untill he provided the details of my son as what is his name and where he is serving etc.
When my wife read the FIR he asked the police officer that it was an attempt to murder and as per medical record of heritage hospital and rasra hospital he has sign of 18 wounds on his body 2 fracture beside his left eye and on fracture on his hand. The officer told that what we have written is right we have seen everything
On the next day my wife approached to sp ballia and told him about the matter and when sp ballia asked him he told that the medical documents to bharat tiwari is not received from heritage hospital Varanasi as soon as the medical documents will be received we will increase the required ipc sections.
My son immediately contacted with administration of heritage hospital to take the medicolegal documents but the officials of heritage hospital refused to give the documents as it was a case of fighting. He told my son to give application to police station rasra and police will come to receive the original documents
My wife immediately gave a written application to SHO Rasra and requested to receive the medical documents and send the same copy to CO Rasra and SP Ballia but till the date my medical documents is not received from heritage hospital by the rasra police.
In between police continued to raid on my home to arrest my family members but everybody was taking treatment in the hospital.
When I discharged from hospital SI Ramashrya Chaudhary came to my home and told me to come to police station as I was accused of ipc 452 but when I showed him the documents of bail granted to me he told me that provide me the duplicate medical documents which is given to you by heritage hospital at the time of discharge and sign it I will take action against the accused.
As I was unable to go to police station I signed the documents and send it to the police station by my wife. SI ramashrya chaudhary took the documents and told my wife to go to home telling that we will take action.
After two days my wife again contacted with SHO Rasra and ask about the progress of the case he told my wife that we cannot take action of duplicate copy of the medical documents police will go to heritage hospital and bring the original documents and then action will be taken but till the time document is not received by the police.
SHO Rasra is neither going to heritage hospital to bring the original documents nor he is sending the chargesheet to the dist court ballia so that we can appeal to court to bring the documents from the hospital.
if SHO Rasra will bring the documents from the court he will be forced to take action and if he will send the chargesheet to the court the court will order to bring the medical documents.
In this way he is saving the accused under some political pressure
From last one year I have given a lot of application to SHO Rasra against vijay and others but three times he arrested me in case of breaching the peace and when I gave the same application on tehsil diwas he submitted false report in the favor of accused.
He never provided me any receipt of my application which I gave him telling that it is not a government record so I cannot provide you the receipt of your application.
Every time when I approached him with my application either he threw my application saying that it is false or he arrested me in case of breaching the peace but never took any strong action against the accused and now the accused attacked on me and my whole family and he is saving the accused.
I ,therefore, request you to please interrupt in the matter and change the investigating police officer of the case and I also request you to investigate the case by any senior police officer who do not belong to Rasra Police Station.

Your’s Faithfully
Bharat Tiwari
